Explanation:
The sentence is a description of the reign of King Chandramā, who is said to have brought peace and prosperity to the kingdom. The phrase "धर्मी फूले फलेंगे" (dharmī phūle phalengē) means "the righteous will flourish", and "और जब तक चन्द्रमा बना रहेगा" (aur jab tak Chandramā bhāra rahēga) means "and until Chandramā reigns". The final phrase "तब तक शान्ति बहुत रहेगी" (tab tak shānti bahut rahēgi) means "and until then peace will prevail".
